This method adds on to the player\textquotesingle{}s exhaustion, which may decrease the player\textquotesingle{}s food level.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em amount} & Amount of exhaustion to add, between 0 and 20 (setting it to 20 will guarantee that at least 1, and at most 4, food points are deducted). See \doxylink{class_food_constants}{Food\+Constants} for cost suggestions. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
